as explain in committee part of the act implement the law enforcement directive and make provision for datum processing by competent authority include police force and the crown prosecution service for law enforcement purpose paragraph of the enforcement directive emphasise that the free flow of personal datum between competent authority for the purpose of the prevention investigation detection or prosecution of criminal offence should be facilitate while ensure high level of protection of personal datum however part of the act contain no provision at all to facilitate the free flow of personal datum between the police and the cps instead it impose burdensome obligation on the police require they to redact personal datum from information transfer to the cps those obligation be only delay and obstruct the expeditious progress of the criminal justice system and be not even mandate by the law enforcement directive the problem have arise due to chapter of part of the act which set out six datum protection principle that apply to data processing by competent authority for law enforcement purpose section state the first data protection principle be that the processing of personal datum for any of the law enforcement purpose must be lawful and fair section state the processing of personal datum for any of the law enforcement purpose be lawful only if and to the extent that it be base on law and either the data subject have give consent to the processing for that purpose or the processing be necessary for the performance of task carry out for that purpose by competent authority the police federation have say that it be unlikely that section will apply in this context it have also say that in the case of the test of whether the processing be necessary be exact require competent authority to apply its mind to the proportionality of process specific item of personal datum for the particular law enforcement purpose in question under section to where the processing be sensitive processing an even more rigorous test apply require among other thing that the processing be strictly necessary for the law enforcement purpose in question section state the third data protection principle be that personal datum process for any of the law enforcement purpose must be adequate relevant and not excessive in relation to the purpose for which it be process for the purpose of the act the crown prosecution service and each police force be separate competent authority and separate datum controller therefore as set out in section the cps and each police force must comply with the data protection principle transfer of information by police force to the cps amount to the processing of personal datum the test of necessary and strictly necessary under the first and third datum protection principle require competent authority to identify and consider each and every item of personal datum contain within the information that it be intend to process and to consider whether it be necessary for that item of personal datum to be process in the manner intend the impact of this be that when prepare case file for charge decision from the cps the police must spend huge amount of time and resource analyse information that have be gather by investigate officer in order to identify every item of personal datum they then have to decide whether it be necessary or in many case strictly necessary for the cps to consider each item of personal datum when make its charge decision and to redact every item of personal datum that do not meet that test the national police chiefs council and the cps have produce detailed guidance on this redaction process it emphasise that the act be legal requirement and that the police and the cps do not have any special relationship that negate the need to redact and protect personal information the combination of the requirement of the guidance and of the act represent huge amount of administrative work for police officer result in hour of prepare appropriate redaction furthermore such work be inevitably carry out by relatively junior officer who have no particular expertise in data protection and much of it may never be use by the cps if the matter be not charge or if the defendant plead guilty before trial nationally about of case that be submit to the cps be not charge significant proportion of that time and money could be save if the redaction of personal datum by the police occur after rather than before charge decision have be make by the cps the burden that this be place on police force be highlight in the annual review of disclosure by the attorney general office which hear evidence from police that redaction of material for disclosure be place significant pressure on resource it also find that one police force have invest million in disclosure specialist team solely to deal with redaction in its report on police priority the home affairs committee state the national police chiefs council and the college of policing say this labour intensive process tie up police resource for protect period of time mean investigation take long and possibly add to the likelihood of victim withdraw their support for case the college note that the problem have become bad as digital device such as phone and laptop have develop ever great storage capacity mean there be more datum for the police to process and redact disparity in digital capability across the local force also exacerbate the problem the report go on to say lengthy and inefficient redaction process and protract investigation be neither effective nor fair on either victim or suspect the handling of case file need to comply with data protection law however ensure that the requirement be proportionate and that force have the digital capacity to meet such requirement efficiently be an urgent issue that need address more need to be do to pilot solution and get the balance right furthermore the police federation and the national police chiefs council estimate that the cost nationally of the redaction exercise be over million per annum there be no disputing that there be clear issue here and welcome that this have be acknowledge by ministers have be engage with include the minister for crime policing and fire my right hon friend the member for croydon south chris philp the former home secretary latter emphasise to the government support for reform indeed the autumn statement last week highlight the government commitment to boost public sector productivity by run an ambitious public sector productivity programme with all departments to reimagine the way public service be deliver the focus of that will be on reduce the amount of time our key frontline worker include police doctor and nurse spend on administrative task that be to ensure that they can spend more time deliver for the public arguably the current process of datum redaction be the big unnecessary administrative task keep police officer away from the frontline so reform need to be implement urgently my new clause lay out blueprint for that reform and would insert propose new section into the act to exempt the police service and the cps from comply with the first data protection principle except in so far as that principle require process to be fair or with the third data protection principle when prepare case file for submission to the cps for charge decision thereby facilitate the free flow of personal datum between the police and the cps if the cps decide to charge the case file would be return to the police to carry out the redaction exercise before there be any risk of the file be disclose to any person or body other than the cps in the of case in which the cps decide not to charge the unredacted file would simply be delete by the cps my new clause would have no obvious disadvantage as the security of the personal datum would not be compromise and the necessary redaction would still be undertake once charging decision have be make furthermore provide material unredacted to the cps pre charge would not impact the timeliness of the process in any way as the police would still be provide the same material to the cps as they would have do previously just unredacted know from my conversation with ministers that there be few question from number of source about whether legislative change be the good way to tackle the issue surround redaction to that the police federation have say that the hope be that the cps will set out within their charge advice what material they intend to rely upon and therefore only the require material will have to be redact by the police this would be do in line with the maximum time of service set out within the well case management handbook jan which state that service be require no less than five day before the hearing so we must accept that there may be slight delay in the cps be able to serve their case on the defence at the point of charge but the time in which it will take police force to apply for charge decision to the cps will be far quick without the need for redact thus stop defendant be on bail or under release under investigation status for as long as they currently be and victim of crime wait less time for charge decision in addition the police federation have highlight that while auto redaction software will help to mitigate the current issue it will not recover all policing capacity in respect of redaction officer will still need to review the item to consider what auto redaction parameter need apply otherwise police could risk end up with mass over redaction and have to check to ensure nothing have be miss the real benefit for auto redaction software will come post charge especially if the cps state exactly what material it intend to use or disclose also appreciate that the government feel they can not support my amendment because of three technical legal point and would like to
